   var appendScriptToElement = function(selector, url){
				if(typeof selector !== 'undefined' && typeof url !== 'undefined'){
				var u = url || '',    
					selection = $(selector),
					script = document.createElement( 'script' );
					if((u !== '') && (selection.length === 1)){
						script.type = 'text/javascript';
						script.src = u;
						selection.append(script);
					}    
				}
			};
			var is3rdPartyOptedIn = function() {
			    var cookies = document.cookie.split(';'),
			        i = cookies.length - 1,
			        cookie = {};
			    for (i; i >= 0; i--) {
			        var keyValue = cookies[i],
			            k = keyValue.substring(0, keyValue.indexOf('=')).trim(),
			            v = keyValue.substring(keyValue.indexOf('='), keyValue.length).replace('=', '').trim();
			        if ((k.length > 0) && (v.length > 0)) {
			            if (k === 'tCookie2') {
			                try {
			                    cookie = JSON.parse(v);
			                } catch (e) {}
			                if (('p1' in cookie) && (cookie.p1 === 'true')) {
			                    return true;
			                }
			                break;
			            }
			        }
			    }
			    return false;
			};
			if(is3rdPartyOptedIn()){
				window['optimizely'] = window['optimizely'] || []; 
				window['optimizely'].push(["optOutThirdPartyCookies"]);
